    SELECT TOP(2) [q].[QuizId], [q].[CreatedDate], [q].[QuestionCount], [q].[ShowCase], [q].[Title], [q].[UpdatedDate]

SELECT [q].[QuizId], [q].[CreatedDate], [q].[QuestionCount], [q].[ShowCase], [q].[Title], [q].[UpdatedDate], [t].[DepartmentId], [t].[DepartmentName], [t].[DepartmentsDepartmentId], [t].[QuizzesQuizId]

LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [d0].[DepartmentId], [d0].[DepartmentName], [q1].[DepartmentsDepartmentId], [q1].[QuizzesQuizId]
    FROM [QuizDepartments] AS [q1]
    INNER JOIN [Departments] AS [d0] ON [q1].[DepartmentsDepartmentId] = [d0].[DepartmentId]
) AS [t] ON [q].[QuizId] = [t].[QuizzesQuizId]
WHERE EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM [QuizDepartments] AS [q0]
    INNER JOIN [Departments] AS [d] ON [q0].[DepartmentsDepartmentId] = [d].[DepartmentId]
    WHERE ([q].[QuizId] = [q0].[QuizzesQuizId]) AND ([d].[DepartmentId] = @__departmentId_0)) AND ([q].[ShowCase] = CAST(1 AS bit))
ORDER BY [q].[QuizId], [t].[DepartmentsDepartmentId], [t].[QuizzesQuizId]
